     871             : /************************************************************************/
     872             : 
     873             : CPL_NOSANITIZE_UNSIGNED_INT_OVERFLOW
     874        6000 : static int AddWithOverflowAccepted(int a, int b)
     875             : {
     876             :     // In fact in normal situations a+b should not overflow. That can only
     877             :     // happen with corrupted datasets. But we don't really want to add code
     878             :     // to detect that situation, so basically this is just a trick to perform
     879             :     // the addition without the various sanitizers to yell about the overflow.
     880             :     //
     881             :     // Assumes complement-to-two signed integer representation and that
     882             :     // the compiler will safely cast a big unsigned to negative integer.
     883             :     return static_cast<int>(
     884        6000 :                         static_cast<unsigned>(a) + static_cast<unsigned>(b));
     885             : }
